# Changelog

## [0.0.5](https://github.com/snowdreamtech/UniGo/compare/v0.0.5...v0.0.5) (2026-07-14)


### ⚠ BREAKING CHANGES

* **security:** mise now downloads binaries ONLY from GitHub Releases
* mise does NOT automatically detect musl

### ci

* **dependabot:** add path monitoring for mise toolchain config ([ebc7227](https://github.com/snowdreamtech/UniGo/commit/ebc72273a85cb32f3e66b84305c726e47ce55b63))
* **deps:** remove MISE_SKIP_CHECKSUM workaround ([0a80645](https://github.com/snowdreamtech/UniGo/commit/0a8064500cc0ecef8851af4aea31023f5809512e))

## [0.0.3](https://github.com/snowdreamtech/UniGo/compare/v0.0.3...v0.0.3) (2026-07-05)


### ⚠ BREAKING CHANGES

* **security:** mise now downloads binaries ONLY from GitHub Releases
* mise does NOT automatically detect musl

* **dependabot:** add path monitoring for mise toolchain config ([ebc7227](https://github.com/snowdreamtech/UniGo/commit/ebc72273a85cb32f3e66b84305c726e47ce55b63))
